< review>
Wonderful, professional, quick.

First called to ask questions, they said they acceptes walk-ins and gave me a straightforward quote right away.

Walked in, dropped off one phone (Samsung Galaxy S7) for a back of phone glass (not screen) and they helped my mother replace the glass screen protector on her iPhone 6+ (which he didn't have to, after selling it to her). We were in and out in less than 10 minutes, with a quote for the s7.

They called no more than 2 hours later to come pick the S7 up, even though they looked somewhat busy earlier. Quote was exactly what I paid, and it looked brand new.

The employee who helped me even moved the metal plate from my old back to the new back, free of charge. The plate is a part of the magnetic Schoche phone holder for my car. I was under the impression that I would have to buy a new one, but he removed it, and placed it back on for me! Above and beyond what I asked for. They could have easily charged me for a new one, or gotten a few bucks out of me for that.

All in all, professional, quick, reliable, and an inexpensive fix to extend the life of my phone, and my mother's phone. Highly recommended.< /review>

Phenomenal NY Style Bagels.  The Garlic and Poppy were just perfect.  The great crust on the outside protects the soft, chewy center.  The 2nd picture is of the lox and cream cheese.  The salmon was the best we've had on this one-month road trip around Southern California.

<Resp>None</Resp>< review>
Manhattan Bread & Bagel is small but well loved by locals. The fresh bread is fantastic, and morning bagels are always tasty. The sandwich menu stays the same, but is good with staples that work well. My favourite is the BBQ BLT!

Fresh cookies are always a welcome (and totally worth it!) temptation. They also have packaged salads that are a snap to pick up and roll with - these salads are surprisingly crisp, full and tasty.

Pro tip - if you bring your kids (or if you're feeling nostalgic), get the PB&J with the crust cut off and a cold whole milk. It's awesome!<//review>

< Text>
I love the bagels and cream cheese here, and the coffee is good. Plus, they have other choices such as sandwiches with egg, cheese, bacon, and such. However, I feel that the cream cheese is somewhat overpriced. So I don't come here too often, unless I want to give myself a special treat! Sometimes, if I'm waiting to have my car serviced at Firestone Complete Auto Care Center down the block on Sepulveda, and I'm not planning to go home while my car is being serviced, I will walk to Manhattan Bread & Bagel to grab a bagel and a cream cheese tub. Admittedly, I like a lot of bagel with my cream cheese, if you get my drift! I do want to mention that the service here is a little bit inconsistent in terms of the attitude of the servers. Not long ago, one of them was not friendly or courteous at all. But, in general, it's fine for the treats that it's known for!< /Text>

1489642731479< /Time>
< rating>
4</rating>
< Text>
This place is funky looking, and the cashier / server / owner(?) is a little cranky and moody, but when you've come in a few times and know what you want, he warms up quite a lot. The portion sizes are great! Another reviewer mentioned that the food quality was "just ok". I have news for you...its Hawaiian BBQ!!! There is lots of sugar in the BBQ sauce, they have white rice and mac salad (mac an mayo)...that's what Hawaiian BBQ kind of is! The prices are great, the portion sizes are great (shredded pork and cabbage (you have to ask for the cabbage, and it costs a bit extra, but its worth it!) is excellent and its enough for two or three meals. This is a hidden gem in El Cerrito if what you want is real, good Hawaiian BBQ and don't mind that it hasn't been repainted in a while and sometimes is a bit drafty. Its not a place for a fine dining experience, but it's real Hawaiian BBQ!!</Text>

It was more like $30 all together with the $20 lock and taxes. Still doable though.  I signed a contract that was agreeing to all kinds of stupid fees. I didn't care,  I need speed service and empty cars. Deangelo was in the office doing his job,  crossing T's and dotting i's. He was very efficient. It was obvious that there is a procedure he was loyal to following. I appreciate employees like that because they are representing their company by design.
My concern is the design!!!!!

Don't rent from Public Storage on Federal Blvd if:
You work during the day and want to be able to get to your things before or after work.  THEIR HOURS are 9:30-6pm to get into your unit.

Don't rent from Public Storage on Federal Blvd if:
You don't have an EXIT PLAN that has you moving out before the first full month payment.
Because they have a plan.

Don't rent from Public Storage on Federal Blvd if:
You aren't someone good at reading the FINE PRINT print. They have a $30 late payment fee, due the DAY BEFORE you've been there a month. Then a $55 lien fee. A $7.50 going to auction fee. When they auction your unit they charge another fee around $130 for auctioning your unit.  Whatever they don't get in the auction, you still owe and it goes on YOUR  CREDIT!

Don't rent from Public Storage on Federal Blvd if:
You have another option. You don't want a storage unit that your experience becomes one like that of a gambler and a bookie. < Review>
I had just arrived to California on the 18th of November, and was in need of a storage unit to put my belongings that would be arriving in a few days. I first arrived at one location and unfortunately they didn't have the size I needed and they directed me to their other location on 54th street.  When I arrived into the office I was greeted by a young lady name Shawnte. She seemed to be extremely busy but was handling the stress really well.  There was another customer she was helping at the time that needed a unit too. So Shawnte decided to take both of us out at the same time to show us each a unit. Shawnte was accompanied by another I believed to be named Ryan who walked with us. While Shawnte was showing the other gentleman the space, Ryan showed me mine.  They both worked great together. Once we got back to the office Shawnte began to handle all the paper work that's when Marcela had came back from her lunch and jumped in to assist Shawnte. Marcela explained everything very well and answered all my questions. I trust my items are very safe and I would recommend Public Storage to anyone.< /Review>
